\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00651}00651 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00652}00652         npab = real(npa + npb,kind=rk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00653}00653         matmeana(1:nd,1) = meana}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00654}00654         matmeanb(1:nd,1) = meanb}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00655}00655 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00656}00656         \textcolor{comment}{! First find Mean:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00657}00657         mean = ( real(npa,kind=rk)*meana + real(npb,kind=rk)*meanb ) / npab}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00658}00658         matmean(1:nd,1) = mean}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00659}00659 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00660}00660         \textcolor{comment}{! Now find new Covariance matrix:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00661}00661         covmat  = real(npa,kind=rk) * ( covmata + matmul(matmeana,transpose(matmeana)) ) \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00662}00662                 + real(npb,kind=rk) * ( covmatb + matmul(matmeanb,transpose(matmeanb)) )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00663}00663         covmat  = covmat/npab -\/ matmul(matmean,transpose(matmean))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00664}00664 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00685}00685     npabinverse = 1.\_rk / real(npa + npb,kind=rk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00686}00686 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00687}00687     \textcolor{comment}{! First find MeanVec:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00688}00688     meanvec = npabinverse * ( npareal*meanveca + npbreal*meanvecb )}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00690}00690     \textcolor{comment}{! Now find new Covariance matrix:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00691}00691     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} j = 1,nd}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00692}00692       \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1,j}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00693}00693         covmatupper(i,j) = ( npareal * ( covmatuppera(i,j) + meanveca(i) * meanveca(j) ) \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00694}00694                            + npbreal * ( covmatupperb(i,j) + meanvecb(i) * meanvecb(j) ) ) * npabinverse \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00695}00695                          -\/ meanvec(i) * meanvec(j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l00696}00696 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end do}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01509}01509     c = 1.\_rk}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01510}01510     d = 1.\_rk-\/qab*x/qap}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01511}01511     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (abs(d) < fpmin) d = fpmin}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01512}01512     d = 1.\_rk/d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01513}01513     getbetacontinuedfraction = d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01514}01514     \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} m = 1,maxit}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01515}01515       m2 = 2*m}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01516}01516       aa = m*(b-\/m)*x/((qam+m2)*(a+m2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01517}01517       d = 1.\_rk+aa*d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01518}01518       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (abs(d) < fpmin) d = fpmin}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01519}01519       c = 1.\_rk+aa/c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01520}01520       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (abs(c) < fpmin) c = fpmin}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01521}01521       d = 1.\_rk/d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01522}01522       getbetacontinuedfraction = getbetacontinuedfraction*d*c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01523}01523       aa = -\/(a+m)*(qab+m)*x/((a+m2)*(qap+m2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01524}01524       d = 1.\_rk+aa*d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01525}01525       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (abs(d) < fpmin) d = fpmin}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01526}01526       c = 1.\_rk+aa/c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01527}01527       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (abs(c) < fpmin) c = fpmin}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01528}01528       d = 1.\_rk/d}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01529}01529       del = d*c}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01530}01530       getbetacontinuedfraction = getbetacontinuedfraction*del}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01531}01531       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (abs(del-\/1.\_rk) <=  eps) \textcolor{keywordflow}{exit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01532}01532 \textcolor{keywordflow}{    end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01533}01533     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m > maxit) \textcolor{keywordflow}{then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01534}01534       error stop}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{______toBeCleared_______2Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01535}01535       \textcolor{comment}{!call abortProgram( output\_unit , 1 , 1 , 'Statitistics@getBetaContinuedFraction() failed: a or b too big, or maxit too small.' )}}
